NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE.
M. Faridha, aged 23 years (female) who is mentally retarded, daughter of N. MAZHARUDDIN HUSSAIN born
on 3rd February 1990. Residing at 4/153 1st Jayalakshmi Nagar, Shanthoshpuram, Chennai-600 073, shall henceforth
will be known as M. SYED ALI FATHIMA.
Chennai,
2nd January 2014.

N. MAZHARUDDIN HUSSAIN
(Father.)

Form No. 155
(See Rule 329)
Members Voluntary winding up
EAST WEST MEDIA INTERNATIONAL PRIVATE LIMITED
(in liquidation)
Notice convening final meeting
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of section 497 that a General Meeting of the Members of the above
named company will be held at Flat No.7, Rams Flat, No.30, Ramachandra Iyer Street, T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017 on
Friday the 21st February, 2014 at 11 O’ clock in the forenoon for the purpose of having an account laid before them
showing the manner in which the winding-up has been conducted and the property of the company disposed of and hearing
any explanation that may be given by the liquidator and also of determining by a special resolution of the company, the
manner in which the books, accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.
Chennai,
3rd January 2014.

RAMYA RADHAKRISNAN,
Liquidator.
